/app/api/auth/login/route.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/api/auth/login/route.ts
 2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 3 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 6 | import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
 7 | import { LoginDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 8 | import { validateTenant } from '@/lib/server/tenant';
 9 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
10 | 
11 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
12 | 
13 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
14 |   try {
15 |     const tenantId = request.headers.get('x-tenant-id');
16 |     if (!tenantId) {
17 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant required' }, { status: 400 });
18 |     }
19 | 
20 |     // Validate tenant existence
21 |     await validateTenant(tenantId);
22 | 
23 |     const body = await request.json();
24 |     const data = LoginDto.parse(body);
25 | 
26 |     console.log(`[API] Login attempt for tenant: ${tenantId}, email: ${data.email}`);
27 | 
28 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
29 |     const users = await tenantDb.select().from(schema.users).where(eq(schema.users.email, data.email)).limit(1);
30 | 
31 |     if (!users.length) {
32 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
33 |     }
34 | 
35 |     const user = users[0];
36 |     const match = await bcrypt.compare(data.password, user.password);
37 |     if (!match) {
38 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
39 |     }
40 | 
41 |     const token = jwt.sign({ tenantId, userId: user.id }, env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '1h' });
42 | 
43 |     const response = NextResponse.json({ message: 'Login successful' });
44 |     response.cookies.set('authToken', token, { httpOnly: true, secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production', sameSite: 'strict', maxAge: 3600 });
45 |     return response;
46 |   } catch (err) {
47 |     console.error('[API] Login failed:', err);
48 |     if (err instanceof Error && err.message === 'Tenant not found') {
49 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant not found' }, { status: 404 });
50 |     }
51 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal error' }, { status: 500 });
52 |   }
53 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/api/tenants/route.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/api/tenants/route.ts
 2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 3 | import { sharedDb, getTenantDb, executeRawQuery } from '@/lib/db';
 4 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
 5 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 6 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 7 | import { TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 8 | import z from 'zod/v4';
 9 | 
10 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
11 | 
12 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
13 |   try {
14 |     const body = await request.json();
15 |     const data = TenantSignupDto.parse(body);
16 |     const tenantId = data.tenantId; 
17 |     const schemaName = `tenant_${tenantId}`;
18 | 
19 |     console.log(`[API] Creating tenant: ${tenantId}, schema: ${schemaName}`);
20 | 
21 |     const existing = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId));
22 |     if (existing.length) {
23 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant ID already exists' }, { status: 409 });
24 |     }
25 | 
26 |     // Create schema and users table
27 |     await executeRawQuery(`CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS "${schemaName}";`);
28 |     await executeRawQuery(`
29 |       CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "${schemaName}".users (
30 |         id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
31 |         name TEXT NOT NULL,
32 |         email TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
33 |         password TEXT NOT NULL
34 |       );
35 |     `);
36 | 
37 |     // Insert tenant metadata
38 |     await sharedDb.insert(tenants).values({
39 |       tenantId,
40 |       schemaName,
41 |       name: data.orgName,
42 |     });
43 | 
44 |     // Insert admin user
45 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
46 |     const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(data.adminPassword, 12);  // Stronger salt (12 rounds)
47 |     await tenantDb.insert(schema.users).values({
48 |       name: data.adminName,
49 |       email: data.adminEmail,
50 |       password: hashedPassword,
51 |     });
52 | 
53 |     console.log(`[API] Tenant created successfully: ${tenantId}`);
54 |     return NextResponse.json({ message: 'Tenant created', tenantId });
55 |   } catch (err) {
56 |     console.error('[API] Tenant creation failed:', err);
57 |     if (err instanceof z.ZodError) {
58 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: err }, { status: 400 });
59 |     }
60 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal error' }, { status: 500 });
61 |   }
62 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/dashboard/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/dashboard/page.tsx
 2 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
 3 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
 4 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 5 | 
 6 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 7 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 8 | 
 9 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';  // Node runtime
10 | 
11 | export default async function DashboardPage() {
12 |   const cookieStore = cookies();
13 |   const token = (await cookieStore).get('authToken')?.value;
14 |   if (!token) {
15 |     return <div>Unauthorized</div>;
16 |   }
17 | 
18 |   let decoded;
19 |   try {
20 |     decoded = verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as { tenantId: string; userId: number };
21 | 
22 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(decoded.tenantId);
23 |     const user = await tenantDb.select().from(schema.users).where(eq(schema.users.id, decoded.userId)).limit(1);
24 | 
25 |     return (
26 |       <div className="min-h-screen p-8 bg-gray-100">
27 |         <h1 className="text-3xl">Welcome to {decoded.tenantId} Dashboard</h1>
28 |         <p>Email: {user[0]?.email}</p>
29 |       </div>
30 |     );
31 |   } catch (err) {
32 |     if (err === 'Tenant not found') {
33 |       return <div>Tenant not found</div>;
34 |     }
35 |     return <div>Invalid token</div>;
36 |   }
37 | }

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/login/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/login/page.tsx
 2 | 'use client';
 3 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 4 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 5 | import { LoginInput, LoginDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 6 | import { useState } from 'react';
 7 | import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
 8 | 
 9 | export default function LoginPage() {
10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
11 |   const router = useRouter();
12 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<LoginInput>({
13 |     resolver: zodResolver(LoginDto),
14 |   });
15 | 
16 |   const onSubmit = async (data: LoginInput) => {
17 |     const res = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
18 |       method: 'POST',
19 |       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
20 |       body: JSON.stringify(data),
21 |     });
22 |     if (res.ok) {
23 |       router.push('/dashboard');
24 |     } else {
25 |       const result = await res.json();
26 |       setMessage(result.error || 'Login failed');
27 |     }
28 |   };
29 | 
30 |   return (
31 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-800">
32 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-green p-8 rounded shadow-md w-96">
33 |         <h1 className="text-2xl mb-4">Login</h1>
34 |         <input {...register('email')} placeholder="Email" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
35 |         {errors.email && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.email.message}</p>}
36 |         <input type="password" {...register('password')} placeholder="Password" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
37 |         {errors.password && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.password.message}</p>}
38 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-500 text-white p-2 w-full">Login</button>
39 |         <p className="mt-2">{message}</p>
40 |       </form>
41 |     </div>
42 |   );
43 | }

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/signup/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/signup/page.tsx
 2 | 'use client';
 3 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 4 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 5 | import { TenantSignupInput, TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 6 | import { useState } from 'react';
 7 | import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
 8 | 
 9 | export default function SignupPage() {
10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
11 |   const router = useRouter();
12 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<TenantSignupInput>({
13 |     resolver: zodResolver(TenantSignupDto),
14 |   });
15 | 
16 |   const onSubmit = async (data: TenantSignupInput) => {
17 |     const res = await fetch('/api/tenants', {
18 |       method: 'POST',
19 |       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
20 |       body: JSON.stringify(data),
21 |     });
22 |     const result = await res.json();
23 |     if (res.ok) {
24 |       setMessage(`Tenant created! Redirecting to dashboard...`);
25 |       // Redirect to tenant dashboard (add to /etc/hosts first)
26 |       window.location.href = `http://${data.tenantId}.localhost:3000/dashboard`;
27 |     } else {
28 |       setMessage(result.error || 'Error creating tenant');
29 |     }
30 |   };
31 | 
32 |   return (
33 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-800">
34 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-white p-8 rounded shadow-md w-96">
35 |         <h1 className="text-2xl mb-4">Tenant Signup</h1>
36 |         <input {...register('orgName')} placeholder="Organization Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
37 |         {errors.orgName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.orgName.message}</p>}
38 |         <input {...register('tenantId')} placeholder="Tenant ID (e.g., plano-isd)" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
39 |         {errors.tenantId && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.tenantId.message}</p>}
40 |         <input {...register('adminName')} placeholder="Admin Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
41 |         {errors.adminName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminName.message}</p>}
42 |         <input {...register('adminEmail')} placeholder="Admin Email" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
43 |         {errors.adminEmail && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminEmail.message}</p>}
44 |         <input type="password" {...register('adminPassword')} placeholder="Admin Password" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
45 |         {errors.adminPassword && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminPassword.message}</p>}
46 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-500 text-white p-2 w-full">Signup</button>
47 |         <p className="mt-2 text-center">{message}</p>
48 |       </form>
49 |     </div>
50 |   );
51 | }

/components/ui/alert.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import * as React from "react"
 2 | import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
 3 | 
 4 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
 5 | 
 6 | const alertVariants = cva(
 7 |   "relative w-full rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-sm grid has-[>svg]:grid-cols-[calc(var(--spacing)*4)_1fr] grid-cols-[0_1fr] has-[>svg]:gap-x-3 gap-y-0.5 items-start [&>svg]:size-4 [&>svg]:translate-y-0.5 [&>svg]:text-current",
 8 |   {
 9 |     variants: {
10 |       variant: {
11 |         default: "bg-card text-card-foreground",
12 |         destructive:
13 |           "text-destructive bg-card [&>svg]:text-current *:data-[slot=alert-description]:text-destructive/90",
14 |       },
15 |     },
16 |     defaultVariants: {
17 |       variant: "default",
18 |     },
19 |   }
20 | )
21 | 
22 | function Alert({
23 |   className,
24 |   variant,
25 |   ...props
26 | }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & VariantProps<typeof alertVariants>) {
27 |   return (
28 |     <div
29 |       data-slot="alert"
30 |       role="alert"
31 |       className={cn(alertVariants({ variant }), className)}
32 |       {...props}
33 |     />
34 |   )
35 | }
36 | 
37 | function AlertTitle({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
38 |   return (
39 |     <div
40 |       data-slot="alert-title"
41 |       className={cn(
42 |         "col-start-2 line-clamp-1 min-h-4 font-medium tracking-tight",
43 |         className
44 |       )}
45 |       {...props}
46 |     />
47 |   )
48 | }
49 | 
50 | function AlertDescription({
51 |   className,
52 |   ...props

54 |   return (
55 |     <div
56 |       data-slot="alert-description"
57 |       className={cn(

60 |       )}

64 | }

 1 | import * as React from "react"
 2 | import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
 3 | import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
 4 | 
 5 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
 6 | 
 7 | const buttonVariants = cva(
 8 |   "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
 9 |   {
10 |     variants: {
11 |       variant: {
12 |         default:
13 |           "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-primary/90",
14 |         destructive:
15 |           "bg-destructive text-white shadow-xs hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
16 |         outline:
17 |           "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
18 |         secondary:
19 |           "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-secondary/80",
20 |         ghost:
21 |           "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
22 |         link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
23 |       },
24 |       size: {
25 |         default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
26 |         sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
27 |         lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
28 |         icon: "size-9",
29 |       },
30 |     },
31 |     defaultVariants: {
32 |       variant: "default",
33 |       size: "default",
34 |     },
35 |   }
36 | )
37 | 
38 | function Button({
39 |   className,
40 |   variant,
41 |   size,
42 |   asChild = false,
43 |   ...props
44 | }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
45 |   VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
46 |     asChild?: boolean
47 |   }) {
48 |   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"
49 | 
50 |   return (
51 |     <Comp
52 |       data-slot="button"
53 |       className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
54 |       {...props}
55 |     />
56 |   )
57 | }
58 | 
59 | export { Button, buttonVariants }

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/db/index.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/db/index.ts
 2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/node-postgres';
 3 | import { Pool, Client } from 'pg';
 4 | import { pgSchema } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 5 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 6 | import { tenants } from './schema/shared';
 7 | import { usersColumns } from './schema/tenant';
 8 | import { env } from '../../env.mjs';
 9 | 
10 | // Single shared pool for the entire database (all schemas)
11 | const sharedPool = new Pool({ connectionString: env.DATABASE_URL });
12 | export const sharedDb = drizzle(sharedPool);
13 | 
14 | // Function to get tenant-specific DB (dynamic schema qualification, same pool)
15 | export async function getTenantDb(tenantId: string) {
16 |   console.log(`[DB] Resolving tenant DB for ${tenantId}`);
17 |   const tenant = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId)).limit(1);
18 |   if (!tenant.length) {
19 |     console.error(`[DB] Tenant not found: ${tenantId}`);
20 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
21 |   }
22 |   const schemaName = tenant[0].schemaName;
23 | 
24 |   const tenantSchema = pgSchema(schemaName);
25 |   const users = tenantSchema.table('users', usersColumns);
26 | 
27 |   const tenantDb = drizzle(sharedPool, { schema: { users } });
28 |   console.log(`[DB] Tenant DB initialized for schema: ${schemaName}`);
29 |   return { db: tenantDb, schema: { users } };
30 | }
31 | 
32 | // For raw queries (e.g., schema creation)
33 | export async function executeRawQuery(query: string) {
34 |   const client = new Client({ connectionString: env.DATABASE_URL });
35 |   await client.connect();
36 |   try {
37 |     await client.query(query);
38 |     console.log(`[DB] Executed raw query: ${query.substring(0, 50)}...`);
39 |   } finally {
40 |     await client.end();
41 |   }
42 | }
43 | 
44 | // Export types
45 | export type TenantDb = Awaited<ReturnType<typeof getTenantDb>>;

/lib/db/schema/shared.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/db/schema/shared.ts
 2 | import { pgTable, serial, text, timestamp } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 3 | 
 4 | export const tenants = pgTable('tenants', {
 5 |   id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
 6 |   tenantId: text('tenant_id').notNull().unique(),
 7 |   schemaName: text('schema_name').notNull(),
 8 |   name: text('name').notNull(),
 9 |   createdAt: timestamp('created_at').defaultNow().notNull(),
10 | });

5 |   id: serial('id').primaryKey(),

/lib/dto/tenant.ts:

 1 | // lib/dto/tenant.ts
 2 | import { z } from 'zod';
 3 | 
 4 | export const TenantSignupDto = z.object({
 5 |   orgName: z.string().min(3, 'Org name must be at least 3 characters').max(50),
 6 |   tenantId: z.string().min(3, 'Tenant ID must be at least 3 characters').max(50).regex(/^[a-z0-9-]+$/, 'Tenant ID must be lowercase letters, numbers, or hyphens'),
 7 |   adminName: z.string().min(3, 'Admin name must be at least 3 characters').max(100),
 8 |   adminEmail: z.string().email('Invalid email'),
 9 |   adminPassword: z.string().min(8, 'Password must be at least 8 characters'),
10 | });
11 | 
12 | export const LoginDto = z.object({
13 |   email: z.string().email('Invalid email'),
14 |   password: z.string().min(8, 'Password must be at least 8 characters'),
15 | });
16 | 
17 | export type TenantSignupInput = z.infer<typeof TenantSignupDto>;

/lib/server/tenant.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/server/tenant.ts
 2 | import { sharedDb } from '@/lib/db';
 3 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | 
 6 | export async function validateTenant(tenantId: string) {
 7 |   console.log(`[Tenant] Validating tenant: ${tenantId}`);
 8 |   const tenant = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId)).limit(1);
 9 |   if (!tenant.length) {
10 |     console.error(`[Tenant] Invalid tenant: ${tenantId}`);
11 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
12 |   }
13 |   return tenant[0];
14 | }

/middleware.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // middleware.ts
 2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 3 | 
 4 | export async function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
 5 |   const host = request.headers.get('host') || '';
 6 |   const parts = host.split('.');
 7 |   const tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[0] : null;  // e.g., tenant1.localhost:3000 → tenant1
 8 | 
 9 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Host: ${host}, Tenant ID: ${tenantId}`);
10 | 
11 |   // Public routes (no tenant needed) - added '/'
12 |   const pathname = request.nextUrl.pathname;
13 |   if (!tenantId && (pathname === '/' || pathname.startsWith('/signup') || pathname.startsWith('/login') || pathname.startsWith('/api/tenants') || pathname.startsWith('/api/auth'))) {
14 |     return NextResponse.next();
15 |   }
16 | 
17 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Tenant ID found: ${tenantId}`);
18 |   if (!tenantId) {
19 |     console.error('[Middleware] No tenant ID found');
20 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant not found' }, { status: 404 });
21 |   }
22 | 
23 |   // Set tenant context in headers (no validation here)
24 |   const headers = new Headers(request.headers);
25 |   headers.set('x-tenant-id', tenantId);
26 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Setting x-tenant-id header: ${tenantId}`);
27 |   console.log(`[Middleware] headers: ${JSON.stringify(Array.from(headers.entries()))}`);
28 | 
29 |   return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
30 | }
31 | 
32 | export const config = {
33 |   matcher: ['/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)'],
34 | };
